[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | libde265 is an open source implementation of the h.265 video codec. It is written from scratch and has a plain C API to enable a simple integration into other software.
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | 
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | libde265 supports WPP and tile-based multithreading and includes SSE optimizations. The decoder supports all features of the Main and Main10 profile (HEVC-V1) and most profiles of HEVC-V2 (chroma 4:2:2, 4:4:4, monochrome, and bit depths up to 14 bits).

[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | Description:
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | This PPA contains packages to add support for HEIC / HEIF and AVIF files.
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | 
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | libheif is an ISO/IEC 23008-12:2017 HEIF and AVIF (AV1 Image File Format) file format decoder and encoder.
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | 
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | HEIF and AVIF are new image file formats employing HEVC (h.265) or AV1 image coding, respectively, for the best compression ratios currently possible.
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | 
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | libheif makes use of libde265 for HEIF image decoding and x265 for encoding. For AVIF, libaom, dav1d, or rav1e are used as codecs.
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | 
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | libheif has support for decoding
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - tiled images
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - alpha channels
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - thumbnails
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - reading EXIF and XMP metadata
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - reading the depth channel
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - multiple images in a file
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - image transformations (crop, mirror, rotate)
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - overlay images
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - plugin interface to add alternative codecs for additional formats (AVC, JPEG)
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - decoding of files while downloading (e.g. extract image size before file has been completely downloaded)
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - reading color profiles
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - heix images (10 and 12 bit, chroma 4:2:2)
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | 
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | The encoder supports:
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - lossy compression with adjustable quality
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - lossless compression
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - alpha channels
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - thumbnails
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - save multiple images to a file
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - save EXIF and XMP metadata
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - writing color profiles
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - 10 and 12 bit images
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   | - monochrome images
[ubuntu/CI Ubuntu/Ubuntu 24.04 Intel Clang-2]   |
